              <img alt="horizontal rule" cwidth="600" data-orig-height="10" data-orig-width="600" eza="cwidth:600px;;cheight:10px;;wcalc_source:defined;wcalc:600px;wocalc:600px;hcalc:10px;rend_px_area:6000;" src="https://www.religioustolerance.org/topruled.gif" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;width:450px;height:7px;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/p[3]/img;pagepos:623;cwidth:600px;cheight:10px;wcalc_source:defined;wcalc:600px;wocalc:600px;hcalc:10;rend_px_area:6000;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:0;obj_px_area:6000;req_px_area:6000;req_px_height:0;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;parent-line-height:normal;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;"/>

             <h1 align="left" cwidth="877" eza="cwidth:877px;;cheight:39px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:89px;wocalc:89px;hcalc:156px;rend_px_area:34203;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;font-size:32px;font-weight:bold;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/h1;pagepos:624;cwidth:877px;cheight:39px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:89px;wocalc:89px;hcalc:156;rend_px_area:34203;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:103;req_px_area:22214.4;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:41.6;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:42.56;vertical_margin:0;parent-line-height:normal;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              About this web site:
             </h1>
             <h2 align="left" cwidth="877" eza="cwidth:877px;;cheight:29px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:106px;wocalc:106px;hcalc:29px;rend_px_area:25433;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;font-size:24px;font-weight:bold;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/h2[2];pagepos:625;cwidth:877px;cheight:29px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:106px;wocalc:106px;hcalc:29;rend_px_area:25433;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:139;req_px_area:6614.4;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:31.2;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;parent-line-height:normal;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              Location:
             </h2>
             <p align="left" cwidth="877" eza="cwidth:877px;;cheight:60px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:100px;wocalc:100px;hcalc:420px;rend_px_area:52620;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/p[4];pagepos:626;cwidth:877px;cheight:60px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:170px;wocalc:100px;hcalc:420;rend_px_area:52620;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:112;req_px_area:55251;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:32;vertical_margin:0;parent-line-height:normal;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              The group that compiles and maintains this web site is located in Kingston, Ontario, Canada, across Lake Ontario from Rochester, NY. However most of the site's content relates to developments in the United States, where most of its visitors live.
             </p>
             <p align="left" cwidth="877" eza="cwidth:877px;;cheight:60px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:113px;wocalc:113px;hcalc:540px;rend_px_area:52620;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/p[5];pagepos:627;cwidth:877px;cheight:60px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:113px;wocalc:113px;hcalc:540;rend_px_area:52620;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:122;req_px_area:55251;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:32;vertical_margin:0;parent-line-height:normal;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              We are located in the traditional territory of the
              <em cwidth="0" eza="cwidth:0px;;cheight:0px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:54px;wocalc:54px;hcalc:40px;rend_px_area:0;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/p[5]/em;pagepos:629;cwidth:54;cheight:0px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:54px;wocalc:54px;hcalc:40;rend_px_area:0;rcnt:3;ez_min_text_wdth:54;req_px_area:3369.6;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
               Huron-Wendat
              </em>
              and Haudenosaunee Native peoples. The Huron-Wendat are a Native people who speak Iroquoian and occupied the St. Lawrence Valley and estuary to the Great Lakes region in what is now parts of New York State in the U.S., and the provinces of Ontario and Quebec in Canada.
             </p>
             <p align="left" cwidth="877" eza="cwidth:877px;;cheight:40px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:123px;wocalc:123px;hcalc:260px;rend_px_area:35080;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/p[6];pagepos:631;cwidth:877px;cheight:40px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:123px;wocalc:123px;hcalc:260;rend_px_area:35080;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:140;req_px_area:36834;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:32;vertical_margin:0;parent-line-height:normal;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              The term  "Haudenosaunee"  refers to the
              <em cwidth="0" eza="cwidth:0px;;cheight:0px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:90px;wocalc:90px;hcalc:40px;rend_px_area:0;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/p[6]/em;pagepos:633;cwidth:90;cheight:0px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:90px;wocalc:90px;hcalc:40;rend_px_area:0;rcnt:3;ez_min_text_wdth:90;req_px_area:5616;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
               Iroquois Confederacy
              </em>
              comprised of the: Cayuga, Mohawk, Oneida, Onondaga,   Seneca and Tuscarora Nations.
             </p>
             <p align="center" ezoic="wrapper" style="background: transparent; position: static; top: auto; right: auto; left: auto; bottom: auto; -webkit-box-sizing: content-box; background-color: transparent; background-origin: padding-box; background-size: auto; border-spacing: 2px 2px; clear: none; font-family: 'Trebuchet MS', Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; list-style-image: none; list-style-position: outside; list-style-type: disc; text-indent: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; visibility: visible; word-wrap: normal; mcalc: null null null null; pcalc: 0px 0px 0px 0px; nodepath: /html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/p[7]; pagepos: 635; cwidth: 877px; cheight: 10px; wcalc_source: child; wcalc: 600px; wocalc: 600px; hcalc: 10px; rend_px_area: 8770; rcnt: 1; ez_min_text_wdth: ; req_px_area: 6000; height: auto;">
              <img alt="horizontal rule" cwidth="600" data-orig-height="10" data-orig-width="600" eza="cwidth:600px;;cheight:10px;;wcalc_source:defined;wcalc:600px;wocalc:600px;hcalc:10px;rend_px_area:6000;" src="https://www.religioustolerance.org/topruled.gif" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;width:450px;height:7px;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/p[7]/img;pagepos:636;cwidth:600px;cheight:10px;wcalc_source:defined;wcalc:600px;wocalc:600px;hcalc:10;rend_px_area:6000;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:0;obj_px_area:6000;req_px_area:6000;req_px_height:0;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;parent-line-height:normal;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;"/>
             </p>
             <h2 align="left" cwidth="877" eza="cwidth:877px;;cheight:29px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:99px;wocalc:99px;hcalc:29px;rend_px_area:25433;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;font-size:24px;font-weight:bold;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/h2[3];pagepos:637;cwidth:877px;cheight:29px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:99px;wocalc:99px;hcalc:29;rend_px_area:25433;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:124;req_px_area:6177.6;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:31.2;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;parent-line-height:normal;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              Content:
             </h2>
             <blockquote cwidth="797" eza="cwidth:797px;;cheight:348px;;wcalc_source:defined;wcalc:797px;wocalc:797px;hcalc:348px;rend_px_area:277356;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/blockquote;pagepos:638;cwidth:797px;cheight:348px;wcalc_source:defined;wcalc:797px;wocalc:797px;hcalc:348;rend_px_area:277356;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:150;req_px_area:251055;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:83.2;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:128;vertical_margin:0;parent-line-height:normal;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              <p align="left" cwidth="797" eza="cwidth:797px;;cheight:40px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:109px;wocalc:109px;hcalc:280px;rend_px_area:31880;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/blockquote/p[1];pagepos:639;cwidth:797px;cheight:40px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:109px;wocalc:109px;hcalc:280;rend_px_area:31880;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:122;req_px_area:33474;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:32;vertical_margin:0;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
               <span class="Blue" cwidth="0" eza="cwidth:0px;;cheight:0px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:109px;wocalc:109px;hcalc:280px;rend_px_area:0;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;color:rgb(0, 0, 128);nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/blockquote/p[1]/span;pagepos:640;cwidth:109;cheight:0px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:109px;wocalc:109px;hcalc:280;rend_px_area:0;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:109;req_px_area:40809.6;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
                <strong cwidth="0" eza="cwidth:0px;;cheight:0px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:109px;wocalc:109px;hcalc:280px;rend_px_area:0;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;font-weight:bold;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/blockquote/p[1]/span/strong;pagepos:641;cwidth:109;cheight:0px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:109px;wocalc:109px;hcalc:280;rend_px_area:0;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:109;req_px_area:40809.6;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
                 Unlike essentially all other religious web sites, we don't promote the beliefs and practices of a single denomination, faith group, or sect within a single religion.
                </strong>
               </span>
              </p>
              <p align="left" cwidth="797" eza="cwidth:797px;;cheight:80px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:114px;wocalc:114px;hcalc:580px;rend_px_area:63760;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/blockquote/p[2];pagepos:642;cwidth:797px;cheight:80px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:127px;wocalc:114px;hcalc:580;rend_px_area:63760;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:150;req_px_area:66948;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:32;vertical_margin:0;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
               <span class="Blue" cwidth="0" eza="cwidth:0px;;cheight:0px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:127px;wocalc:127px;hcalc:520px;rend_px_area:0;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;color:rgb(0, 0, 128);nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/blockquote/p[2]/span;pagepos:643;cwidth:127;cheight:0px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:127px;wocalc:127px;hcalc:520;rend_px_area:0;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:127;req_px_area:82992;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
                <strong cwidth="0" eza="cwidth:0px;;cheight:0px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:114px;wocalc:114px;hcalc:580px;rend_px_area:0;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;font-weight:bold;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/blockquote/p[2]/span/strong;pagepos:644;cwidth:114;cheight:0px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:114px;wocalc:114px;hcalc:580;rend_px_area:0;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:114;req_px_area:82992;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
                 Instead we try to explain the beliefs, practices, moral teachings and histories of a wide range of faith groups. We promote religious tolerance, freedom, understanding, coexistence, respect, and cooperation. We also promote equal rights and treatment of persons of all  genders, gender identifications, sexual orientations, races, and nationalities.
                </strong>
               </span>
              </p>
              <p align="left" cwidth="797" eza="cwidth:797px;;cheight:120px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:100px;wocalc:100px;hcalc:1180px;rend_px_area:95640;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/blockquote/p[3];pagepos:645;cwidth:797px;cheight:120px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:100px;wocalc:100px;hcalc:1180;rend_px_area:95640;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:122;req_px_area:100422;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:32;vertical_margin:0;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
               Other web sites that discuss religious news generally include only information that has developed in the immediate past -- perhaps during the previous day. This web site often tells  complete stories from beginning to end, sometimes covering a few weeks or even years. An example was the story of the
               <a cwidth="0" eza="cwidth:0px;;cheight:0px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:97px;wocalc:97px;hcalc:100px;rend_px_area:0;" href="mosque-shooting-nz.htm" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;color:rgb(0, 0, 255);nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/blockquote/p[3]/a[1];pagepos:647;cwidth:97;cheight:0px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:97px;wocalc:97px;hcalc:100;rend_px_area:0;rcnt:5;ez_min_text_wdth:97;req_px_area:14123.2;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
                50  murders at two mosques in Christchurch, New Zealand
               </a>
               during 2019-MAR. We covered developments over 17 month's time in five articles. Another was the 2019-APR fire at
               <a cwidth="0" eza="cwidth:0px;;cheight:0px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:71px;wocalc:71px;hcalc:60px;rend_px_area:0;" href="notre-dame%20fire.htm" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;color:rgb(0, 0, 255);nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/blockquote/p[3]/a[2];pagepos:649;cwidth:71;cheight:0px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:71px;wocalc:71px;hcalc:60;rend_px_area:0;rcnt:5;ez_min_text_wdth:71;req_px_area:5907.2;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
                Notre Dame Cathedral
               </a>
               in Paris. We consolidated information from over a dozen news articles published during many months into two articles about the tragedy.
              </p>
              <p cwidth="797" eza="cwidth:797px;;cheight:60px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:98px;wocalc:98px;hcalc:440px;rend_px_area:47820;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/blockquote/p[4];pagepos:651;cwidth:797px;cheight:60px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:98px;wocalc:98px;hcalc:440;rend_px_area:47820;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:122;req_px_area:50211;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:32;vertical_margin:0;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
               According to "
               <em cwidth="0" eza="cwidth:0px;;cheight:0px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:36px;wocalc:36px;hcalc:80px;rend_px_area:0;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/blockquote/p[4]/em;pagepos:653;cwidth:36;cheight:0px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:36px;wocalc:36px;hcalc:80;rend_px_area:0;rcnt:3;ez_min_text_wdth:36;req_px_area:4118.4;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
                The Book Of Odds
               </em>
               ," the probability that a web site  will contain pornography is 1 in 8.3. If you are looking for porn here, you will be disappointed. This web site only has words and the occasional non-pornographic image.
              </p>
             </blockquote>

              Important note:
             </h3>
             <p align="left" cwidth="877" eza="cwidth:877px;;cheight:40px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:93px;wocalc:93px;hcalc:420px;rend_px_area:35080;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/p[10];pagepos:669;cwidth:877px;cheight:40px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:110px;wocalc:93px;hcalc:420;rend_px_area:35080;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:122;req_px_area:36834;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:32;vertical_margin:0;parent-line-height:normal;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">

             </p>
             <p align="center" ezoic="wrapper" style="background: transparent; position: static; top: auto; right: auto; left: auto; bottom: auto; -webkit-box-sizing: content-box; background-color: transparent; background-origin: padding-box; background-size: auto; border-spacing: 2px 2px; clear: none; font-family: 'Trebuchet MS', Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-weight: normal; line-height: normal; list-style-image: none; list-style-position: outside; list-style-type: disc; text-indent: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; visibility: visible; word-wrap: normal; mcalc: null null null null; pcalc: 0px 0px 0px 0px; nodepath: /html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/p[11]; pagepos: 670; cwidth: 877px; cheight: 10px; wcalc_source: child; wcalc: 600px; wocalc: 600px; hcalc: 10px; rend_px_area: 8770; rcnt: 1; ez_min_text_wdth: ; req_px_area: 6000; height: auto;">

             <h3 align="left" cwidth="877" eza="cwidth:877px;;cheight:23px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:109px;wocalc:109px;hcalc:46px;rend_px_area:20171;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;font-size:19px;font-weight:bold;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/h3[2];pagepos:672;cwidth:877px;cheight:23px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:109px;wocalc:109px;hcalc:46;rend_px_area:20171;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:135;req_px_area:8076.9;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:24.7;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;parent-line-height:normal;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              Conventions used:
             </h3>
             <p align="left" cwidth="877" eza="cwidth:877px;;cheight:80px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:100px;wocalc:100px;hcalc:680px;rend_px_area:70160;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/p[12];pagepos:673;cwidth:877px;cheight:80px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:170px;wocalc:100px;hcalc:680;rend_px_area:70160;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:131;req_px_area:73668;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:32;vertical_margin:0;parent-line-height:normal;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              Visitors come to this web site from all over the world. So, we had to select a uniform style for dates. We chose a Year-Month-Day sequence, like 2021-FEB-17, which is rarely used elsewhere, but has the advantage of being clear and unambiguous. If we had used a convention like 04-11-20 then some visitors would read this as April 11, 2020 and others would decode it as NOV-04, 2020.
             </p>
             <p align="left" cwidth="877" eza="cwidth:877px;;cheight:40px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:95px;wocalc:95px;hcalc:240px;rend_px_area:35080;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/p[13];pagepos:674;cwidth:877px;cheight:40px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:110px;wocalc:95px;hcalc:240;rend_px_area:35080;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:122;req_px_area:30888;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:32;vertical_margin:0;parent-line-height:normal;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              To designate years, rather than use the AD/BC convention which is Christian in origin, we use the newer universal designations:
             </p>
             <ul cwidth="837" eza="cwidth:837px;;cheight:80px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:116px;wocalc:116px;hcalc:660px;rend_px_area:66960;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/ul[1];pagepos:675;cwidth:837px;cheight:80px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:116px;wocalc:116px;hcalc:660;rend_px_area:66960;minimum_paddings:0px 0px 0px 40px;minimum_margins:0px 0px 0px 0px;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:94;req_px_area:61839.4;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:41.6;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;parent-line-height:normal;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 40px; padding: 0px 0px 0px 30px; ">
              <li cwidth="837" eza="cwidth:837px;;cheight:60px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:76px;wocalc:76px;hcalc:440px;rend_px_area:50220;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/ul[1]/li[1];pagepos:676;cwidth:837px;cheight:60px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:76px;wocalc:76px;hcalc:440;rend_px_area:50220;minimum_paddings:0px 0px 0px 0px;minimum_margins:0px 0px 0px 0px;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:94;req_px_area:44262.4;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
               CE is equivalent to AD and refers to the "Common Era:" dates that run from 1, when the Jewish prophet, Jesus, was about five years of age, to today, and beyond into the future.
               <br/>
               <br/>
              </li>
              <li cwidth="837" eza="cwidth:837px;;cheight:20px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:76px;wocalc:76px;hcalc:220px;rend_px_area:16740;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/ul[1]/li[2];pagepos:678;cwidth:837px;cheight:20px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:76px;wocalc:76px;hcalc:220;rend_px_area:16740;minimum_paddings:0px 0px 0px 0px;minimum_margins:0px 0px 0px 0px;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:94;req_px_area:17577;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
               BCE is equivalent to BC. It refers to dates "Before the Common Era."  that run before 1 CE.
              </li>
             </ul>

             <h3 align="left" cwidth="877" eza="cwidth:877px;;cheight:29px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:83px;wocalc:83px;hcalc:290px;rend_px_area:25433;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;font-size:19px;font-weight:bold;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/h3[3];pagepos:907;cwidth:877px;cheight:29px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:115px;wocalc:83px;hcalc:290;rend_px_area:25433;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:98;req_px_area:26704.65;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:31.2;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;parent-line-height:normal;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              <b cwidth="0" eza="cwidth:0px;;cheight:0px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:115px;wocalc:115px;hcalc:232px;rend_px_area:0;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/h3[3]/b;pagepos:908;cwidth:115;cheight:0px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:115px;wocalc:115px;hcalc:232;rend_px_area:0;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:98;req_px_area:31075.2;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:31.2;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">

                Visitors come to to this web site from around the world:
               </font>
              </b>
             </h3>
             <p cwidth="877" eza="cwidth:877px;;cheight:100px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:97px;wocalc:97px;hcalc:640px;rend_px_area:87700;" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/p[16];pagepos:910;cwidth:877px;cheight:100px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:97px;wocalc:97px;hcalc:640;rend_px_area:87700;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:112;req_px_area:76388;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:32;vertical_margin:0;parent-line-height:normal;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
              Most visitors come from the U.S. Many others come from the UK, Canada,  Central America,  Scandanavian countries, Central Europe, India, etc.
              <br/>
              <br/>
              We have never been able to figure  out
  who the various isolated folks are, who
              <font cwidth="0" eza="cwidth:0px;;cheight:0px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:38px;wocalc:38px;hcalc:40px;rend_px_area:0;" face="Trebuchet MS,Arial,Helvetica" style="background-color:transparent;background-size:auto;font-family:'Trebuchet MS', Arial, Helvetica;nodepath:/html/body/table/tr/td[3]/table/tr/td/p[16]/font;pagepos:912;cwidth:40;cheight:0px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:40px;wocalc:38px;hcalc:40;rend_px_area:0;rcnt:3;ez_min_text_wdth:38;req_px_area:2912;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:20.8;req_margin_and_padding:0;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">
               seem to be
              </font>
              floating in the southern Pacific Ocean, Indian ocean, near Madagascar, etc.
             </p>

Unfortunately, the U.S. - Canadian border -- the longest undefended border in the world -- is now closed because of the COVID-19 pandemic. Since our office is in Canada, we are no longer able to travel to our U.S. post office box.  Anything that you send there will not be read or answered until the border is reopened. However, the Post Office is saving all incoming material for a time when the border is once more open.
